[2;36m                    [0m         [39mviolation.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow is reproducible with a single test input run [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m times under the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_from_data_fuzzer.cc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is merely exercising the EXIF [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing APIs; the root overflow lies in the core library.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Relevant Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. exif-utils.c — implementation of `exif_get_slong` and `exif_get_long`, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincluding buffer length checks and endianness handling.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. exif-mnote-data-fuji.c — the function `exif_mnote_data_fuji_load`, which calls[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe offending routines when parsing Fuji maker notes.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. exif-data.c — data loading and memory allocation paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_data_load_data`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_new_from_data`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that supply the buffer to `exif_get_slong`.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_from_data_fuzzer.cc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m — entry point demonstrating how [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed EXIF input reaches the vulnerable code.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
